[PHua Fang Lighter Sunk in Collision>

Japanese Soldiers Deny Responsibility for the Accident

Loss of Four Thousand Taels

The Hua Fang lighter of the Hua Fang Lighter Transportation Company on Sichuan Road, towed a steel-hulled lighter, loaded with eight hundred barrels of white powder, from the Wusongkou into the Huangpu River on the evening of the day before yesterday (29th) at around 9:00 PM, to unload cargo at the Yitaixing Wharf. While passing the river surface of the Asiatic Petroleum Wharf, a Japanese soldier's lighter, Fengtian Maru, suddenly came directly from the west to the east. The captain of the Hua Fang lighter saw this and quickly reversed to avoid it, but it was too late, causing the bow of the lighter to be instantly destroyed, and the entire ship sank. The captain, sailors, coolies, and more than ten other people all escaped safely, and the steel lighter was also unharmed. After the captain reported to the company, he immediately reported it to the Yangshupu Water Patrol Station, who sent officers to inspect the scene. The company then negotiated with the Japanese Navy Department yesterday afternoon, but it was closed for Saturday afternoon, and no one could be contacted, so they changed it to Monday for negotiation. It is said that the loss of the lighter is about more than four thousand taels.

Shanghai War Zone Refugee Relief Association Continues to Receive Large Donations

The Provisional Refugee Relief Association in the war zone of this city has rescued a large number of refugees in this war zone, and has set up more than 30 shelters, with more than 300,000 refugees successively. The cost of food and transportation for refugees in the past three or four months has been enormous. People from all walks of life have seen that the association's relief work has been extremely hard-working, and they have all enthusiastically donated. Now it has received 600 yuan in silver dollars raised by Zhou Shizhi, and the Hubei Rescue Shanghai War Zone Refugee Fundraising Office has continued to donate 15,000 silver dollars to help the association.

Renji Charity Hall Resumes Providing Medical Care and Medicine

The Renji Charity Hall on Sixth Malu has always been running various charities, and its medical care and medicine provision is the best in Shanghai. Previously, due to the outbreak of the war, the Provisional Refugee Relief Association in the war zone borrowed the hall to handle affairs, and it was temporarily suspended. Now that summer is approaching, more and more poor people are seeking medical treatment. It is said that the hall will resume providing medical care and medicine as usual from May 2nd. The medical director of the hall is Mr. Ying Tang, and the director is Mr. Ma Jiren.

Detectives Bravely Act, No Thief Escapes

Two Killed...Two Captured Alive...One Wounded by Gunfire

At 7:20 PM on April 29th, five bandits, Zhang Jinkuan, Jiang Chang'an, Zheng Haiqing, Zhou San, and Jin Dasanzi, all from Jiangbei, broke into the home of Zhu Longhai at No. 426 Maigen Road, armed with weapons. Zheng suddenly took out a pistol, threatening them to remain silent, and drove Zhu Longhai and others into a room, monitoring their movements, and then carried out a robbery. At that time, Zhu's co-residents, Xi Dongsheng and Xu Hongsheng, took the opportunity to sneak out and secretly report to Chinese detective Gao Huixian, who reported to the Gordon Road Patrol Station. The patrol captain immediately dispatched Chinese detective chief Shen Chongli, patrolmen Liang Yuliang, Li Baichuan, and Liu Chunshu, and Western detective chief Crawford Elder in three groups to the area. Two groups were ambushed on the nearby north-south thoroughfares, and the opposite side was not guarded because it was a riverbank. Another group, led by Detective Elder, rushed into the gate. At that time, the bandits had already robbed 60 silver dollars and 15 cents, and were about to leave with the loot when they encountered the detectives. The bandit Zheng took out a Mauser pistol and attempted to resist arrest. The detectives took preemptive action and opened fire with their pistols. For a time, the gunfire was as dense as a string of pearls. Zheng was shot three times and fell to the ground. The Mauser pistol and 23 bullets were seized. Zhou died on the spot after being shot and was lying on his side in the owner's room. The bandit Jin Dasanzi was also shot several times and endured the pain to rush out of the gate with the bandit Zhang. Jin fell into the river in front due to his haste and died. The bandit Zhang was also arrested by Detective Shen. Another bandit, Jiang Chang'an, was arrested in the stove shed. In this battle, the two bandits Zhou and Jin were killed on the spot, and some of the original loot of 29 yuan and 75 cents was found near their bodies. The bandit Zheng was wounded by gunfire, and the two bandits Zhang and Jiang were captured alive. The deceased were carried to the Forensic Examination Office on Feilun Road, and the wounded were taken to the hospital for treatment. Zhang and Jiang were taken to the patrol station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the criminal court of the First Special District Court. According to the lawyer of the patrol station, Wang Yaotang, who stated the above situation, the detective Li Baichuan also had a gunshot wound on his leg at the time. However, the patrol station has not yet investigated whether the bandits opened fire to resist arrest, so he requested a postponement. After Judge Wu Tingqi checked and reported, he briefly questioned the two defendants, Zhang and Jiang, and instructed them to be detained for a postponed hearing after investigation. Until about 10:00 AM, Inspector Guo Wei of the Special Court came to the scene to examine the corpses and took the public seat. According to Zhu Longhai, the owner of the house, who claimed to be from Pudong and was running a meat stall, he saw four bandits entering the room last night, one holding a pistol, and confining him and others in a room to carry out the robbery. He pointed out that the captured bandit Jiang Chang'an was indeed at the scene. Guo then issued an order that the two bandits Zhou San and Jin Dasanzi had been confirmed to have resisted arrest before their deaths and were shot and killed on the spot by the detectives. The pistol and 23 bullets were temporarily handed over to the patrol station for safekeeping, and the corpses were handed over to the Binshan Villa for collection.

[PCompardore Borrows Money in the Name of a Foreign Firm>

Resigns on Pretext and Disregards the Debt

Sued by the Foreign Firm on Criminal Charges

Chen Yuru, a compradore from Suzhou who worked for the Jiali Foreign Firm at No. 105 Jiangxi Road, borrowed 14,000 taels from the China Industrial Bank between April 30th of last year, using the name of the firm. At the end of October, he resigned on a pretext and ignored the debt, secretly using the money for his own purposes. The bank reported this to the General Patrol Station, which sent Chinese detective Lai Yuanshan to No. 1659 Huajiangxi Road to arrest him. He was detained in the First Special District Court on charges of theft. Yesterday morning, Judge Jiang opened the court for questioning. The plaintiff's lawyer presented the loan document for investigation and questioned the defendant. The defendant confessed that he had pledged the money on behalf of a customer and had not used it privately, and that he was now willing to settle it gradually. He also hired a lawyer to argue that this was a civil matter and requested to be released on bail to find a way to pay off the debt. The plaintiff's attorney stated that he did not object to bail and asked the court to set a reasonable amount. The defendant paid a surety of 14,000 taels and the hearing was postponed for further verification.

[LImportant Domestic News

Legislative Yuan Discusses Postal Rate Issue

Submitting a Written Inquiry to the Executive Yuan

The Sino-Japanese Issue Was Also Discussed Yesterday

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan discussed the postal rate increase proposal today. The Director of the Postal Department of the Ministry of Communications attended the meeting to report that the increase was necessary for the safety and rapid development of the postal service. Last year's total revenue was 30 to 40 million, but due to the opening of the savings bureau and the impact of the flood, there was a loss of 4 million. It is estimated that the price increase will increase revenue by 10 to 20 million next year. Wei Haosheng said that if the Ministry of Communications increased postal rates for the purpose of building houses and opening savings bureaus, it would be inappropriate. Wang Yongbin said that regardless of whether the price increase issue was reasonable, the Ministry of Communications had violated government orders. On September 1 of last year, the National Government clearly ordered that the central and local governments should first obtain the decision of the Central Political Conference and the review of the Legislative Yuan for the principle of compulsory collection from the people and the granting of special interests such as various exclusive purchases, monopolies, and franchises before they could be established. Since this case has not been discussed by the Central Political Conference or reviewed by this Yuan, the Executive Yuan has no right to independently decide the date of implementation. In addition, the general budget for the 20th year of the Republic has been clearly announced. As a result, Chen Changheng drafted a written inquiry to be sent to the Executive Yuan to instruct the Ministry of Communications to immediately stop implementation. (30th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held its 183rd meeting at 8:00 AM on the 30th. The attending committee members were Zhu Hezhong, the 30th person, and the chairman was Acting President Qin Zhen. The discussion items are as follows: (1) The Legal System Committee of this Yuan reported on the interpretation of the term "net profit" in the Regulations on the Supervision of Private Public Utilities and the limit of public reserve fund deposits. It was resolved to pass the review report. (2) Committee members Cai Xuan, Chen Zhaoying, Zhuang Songfu, Ma Yinchu, and Lin Bin of this Yuan reported on the review of the draft organizational charter of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Regional Fisheries Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Industry. It was resolved to return it to the original reviewers and committee members Wei Tingsheng, Feng Zhaoyi, Zhu Heping, Zhou Wei, and Zhang Mojun for review. (3) Review the Budget Law. (30th Central News Agency Dispatch) (Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan announced this morning that the increase in inland postal rates was illegal. [PMa Zhanshan Declares That He Never Signed a Treaty with Japan

Heihe Ma Zhanshan telegraphed, "All newspaper offices are informed, the Japanese aggression in the Northeast, cunning conspiracy, have emerged repeatedly. The most cruel thing is to force signatures on unilaterally drafted treaties and contracts, which is a habitual trick. The people of the country should be able to understand this. I am only worried that the Japanese will falsely use my name, or coerce other officials remaining in the province, to sign a contract. Therefore, I hereby declare that Heilongjiang has never signed a treaty with Japan. Military Affairs Commission Reforms Army Organization

(Nanjing) In order to standardize the organization of the army, the Military Affairs Commission has decided to reform the organization of divisions. According to the new organizational plan, each division will be divided into two brigades and four regiments, with one battalion each of cavalry and artillery. Each regiment will have four battalions, each battalion will have three infantry companies and one machine gun company, with 135 soldiers per company. The total strength of each division will be approximately 10,000 men. It is planned to begin the reorganization with the troops stationed in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. (Special dispatch on the 30th)

Foreign News Summary

Disarmament Conference Runs Aground

Political Problems Remain Unresolved

Technical Discussions are Futile

Talks Among Five Major Powers Scheduled to Resume Within Two Weeks

Debate Between Germany and France Over Pocket Battleship Issue

Brüning Departs for Berlin

Geneva, April 29 (National News Agency) It was announced here tonight that the General Commission of the Disarmament Conference will not reconvene until the major powers have reached some concrete agreement on certain political issues. This news was released during a conversation between the French representative, Mr. Paul-Boncour, and representatives of the French press. However, Mr. Paul-Boncour still stated that the specialized committees are not adjourning. The chairman of the Disarmament Conference, Mr. Henderson, also issued a similar statement after today's closed-door meeting of the Steering Committee, declaring that the General Commission will not reconvene for the time being, but that everything else will continue as usual without any changes. He also stated that no motion for the complete adjournment of the Disarmament Conference has been proposed. However, it is reliably learned that the complete adjournment of the Disarmament Conference has already been secretly considered by key figures in the conference. Mr. Stimson and Mr. MacDonald both support this move, believing that technical discussions are futile when there is no hope of agreement on political issues. Furthermore, all parties here tonight acknowledge that the Disarmament Conference has run aground because the politicians of the major powers have failed to reach an agreement on political issues. The reason why the major powers have failed to reach an agreement is that Tardieu is unwilling to come to Geneva to allow Britain and America to arbitrate the dispute between France and Germany. If it were not for Mr. Henderson's vigorous opposition to adjournment, the Disarmament Conference might have closed today. However, given the current situation, it is believed that the complete adjournment of the conference is only a matter of time. Whether the conference can avert disaster in the future depends entirely on the resumption of talks among the five major powers. According to British sources, the French government has expressed its willingness to continue the Geneva talks after May 15. Mr. Paul-Boncour's conversation also indicated that talks among the representatives of the five major powers are unlikely to resume before May 12. If this is the case, then it is expected that the Disarmament Conference will have to be postponed until the beginning of June before there is hope of reconvening. One thing is now certain: when the five major powers reopen talks in the future, the US Secretary of State will not be able to participate. Mr. Gibson will represent the United States at that time. According to a member of the US delegation, Mr. Gibson is also very capable of carrying out the United States' proposals. Mr. Stimson will go to an Italian port to take the next mail ship back to the United States. Mr. Stimson originally intended to travel through a French port, but because Mr. Tardieu is unwilling to come to Geneva, Mr. Stimson is also unwilling to go to Paris, and has therefore changed his route through Italy. Therefore, it is recognized here that this matter is tit-for-tat and worthy of investigation.

Geneva, April 29 (National News Agency) After consultations with key figures such as British Prime Minister MacDonald and US Secretary of State Stimson today, it was decided that the disarmament talks among the five major powers would resume within two weeks.

Geneva, April 29 (National News Agency) In today's meeting of the Naval Committee of the Disarmament Conference, the German and French representatives again engaged in a heated debate over pocket battleships. The French representative pointed to the German pocket battleship Deutschland as the most dangerous weapon in the world and argued that it should be abolished. The German representative stood up to refute this, calling it an excellent model of a defensive weapon. He said that if other countries could imitate it, it would save a lot of military spending. As for the fact that its firepower is huge and its armor is thin, this is because the Treaty of Versailles limited Germany to building ships of no more than 10,000 tons, so it had to increase firepower and speed.

Geneva, April 29 (Reuters) At today's meeting of the Naval Committee of the Disarmament Conference, the German representative, Mr. Rheinbaben, said, "The construction cost of a 'pocket battleship' is about half that of a capital ship, but if all countries are willing to reduce the total tonnage of capital ships, then Germany will not hesitate to sacrifice its 'pocket battleship.'" The German representative also said that capital ships are often used to blockade seaports, and therefore indirectly have an offensive function. This function increases or decreases depending on the tonnage. The Japanese representative said that the nature of all combat items should be determined by their use. Capital ships are an important part of the navy, but if they are used to attack the other side, they must rely on other warships to be used at the same time. The US representative, Mr. Swanson, stated that the United States has the responsibility to protect the safety of the Panama Canal and that capital ships are a major element of the US Navy. If they are abolished, then the US defense must be completely reorganized. The British representative, Rear Admiral Pound, said that he agreed with the US representative's opinion that capital ships are only defensive in nature. The British representative also said that he doubts whether capital ships can destroy land-based forts.

Geneva, April 29 (National News Agency) After a final long talk with US Secretary of State Stimson and British Prime Minister MacDonald, German Chancellor Brüning departed for Berlin today. The German Ambassador to France, Mr. Hoesch, came to Geneva to report on a certain issue to the Chancellor and also traveled with him. However, after arriving in Basel, Mr. Hoesch will change trains and return to Paris.

French General Election, First Round of Voting Today

Paris, April 20 (Reuters) Tomorrow is the date for the French Chamber of Deputies election. There are 3,617 candidates for the 615 seats in the Chamber. This is widely regarded as the most important election since the European War. It is anticipated that there will not be major changes among the four major parties, as all parties, with the exception of the Social Revolutionary Party and the extreme conservative party, have largely converged on the main lines of domestic and international policy. If there are changes, it is likely that the Central Party and the Radical Party will gain the position of the extreme source. As there are five or six candidates competing for each seat, a candidate must win an absolute majority of the votes to win. It is expected that at most two or three hundred people will be elected in the first round of voting. The remainder will be elected in the second round of voting on May 8, at which time the parties will negotiate to reduce the number of candidates. The current number of seats held by the four major parties in the Chamber is as follows: National Party 85 seats, Central Group 235 seats, Radical Party 109 seats, Social Party 111 seats. This election campaign has proceeded very quietly, almost unprecedented in French political history, which proves that the constituencies are all aware of the importance of their responsibilities.

(4) Regarding the resolution of the General Assembly on March 11, the Japanese government opposed it by reserving the right to abstain, arguing that the resolution has no binding force, but other countries do not recognize Japan's attitude. They will insist that the March 10 resolution is valid. If this is the case, Japan's opinion and the League of Nations' claim are incompatible, and future disputes are inevitable. Therefore, Japan's presence in the League of Nations is not a good strategy. (5) If the organization of the League of Nations does not change its current state, Japan's resistance to the League of Nations will never end. In addition, this time, in order to protect their own security, the small countries want to deal with the abstract issue of a security guarantee formula in a realistic way. In the future, they will inevitably use the same means against Japan. As a result, Japan's presence in the League of Nations is harmful and useless. (6) Many of our people are worried that if the Shanghai issue is not resolved quickly, the Manchurian issue will also be in a disadvantageous position. The Tragic Death of Lu San in the Lawsuit for Being Wrongfully Accused of Kidnapping After Being Sued for Debt

Detective Zhou is Accused of Murdering Him

Zhou Vehemently Denies Everything

The Nurse Also Testifies in Court

Zhou Honglin, a detective from the General Investigation Office of the General Police Department, together with Detective Chief Lu Liankui and others, took the wanted criminal Chen Sanwenzi in three cars to investigate the kidnappers on Ximen Road in the French Concession on September 28 last year. After passing the west side of the Great World, a person in a rickshaw came face to face. According to the report of the informant who went with them, the person in the rickshaw was the kidnapper Lu San, also known as Lu Qingcai, so they got out of the car and arrested Lu. Unexpectedly, Lu suddenly fell ill a few days later. The police department sent him to the hospital for treatment, but he died. Afterwards, his wife Lu Yin filed a criminal self-accusation with the First Special District Local Court through a lawyer, accusing Zhou Honglin of murdering her husband. It has been tried several times and has been reported in previous newspapers. The court opened again yesterday, but the presiding judge has been replaced by Judge Qian Hongye, so it must be retried. The defendant, Zhou Honglin, hired lawyers Fan Gang and others to defend him. Judge Qian immediately ordered the plaintiff Lu Yin to state the intent of the prosecution. According to her statement, the defendant Zhou Honglin had borrowed 1,000 yuan from her husband in the past and had a written note. When the agreed date arrived, he did not repay the debt. On August 17th of the lunar calendar last year, her husband took the note and went to Zhou to demand payment, and was arrested and accused of being a kidnapper. When her husband was in the hospital, she went to visit him. At that time, he whispered to her that he had been injured by Zhou, and told her to seek justice for him. At that time, no one in the hospital heard him, only Lu Su, who went with her, heard him. Chen Zhu had also witnessed her husband being tortured in the police station. Zhou Honglin, the defendant, stated that Lu Qingcai was arrested by Deputy Detective Tang Jian. Tang Jian searched him on the spot and then transferred him to the Laozha Police Station for detention. Although the case was handled by me, I never independently conducted an investigation of Lu. Since I have been serving in the police station, I have done my best to catch thieves. This time, I have been maliciously accused and intend to retaliate, so the plaintiff's statement is mostly castles in the air and cannot be believed, and so on. Then, Chen Sanwenzi was brought up to testify. Deputy Detective Tang also reported the circumstances of Lu San's arrest, stating that after Lu was taken into the car, the informant confirmed that he was the right person. The nurse, surnamed Lu, was also summoned to the case. According to her statement, Lu Qingcai was very ill at the time, and when he saw his wife, he shook his head frequently, as if refusing people to come near, and she did not see the two parties talking. Judge Qian announced that he would wait for a scheduled debate because the witnesses had already been examined.

Married Daughter Accuses Her Brother

Her Husband Represents Her in Court

Xu Qingyun Forbade Lawsuits Before His Death

Still Inevitably Meet in Court

—A Dispute Between More Than 10 Million and More Than 1 Million—

Fang Xu Meiying, the daughter-in-law of Ningbo businessman Fang Jiyang, and the daughter of the late comprador of the British Bank, Xu Qingyun, hired a lawyer last winter to file a criminal lawsuit in the Second Special District Local Court against her elder brother Xu Maotang for encroaching on the inheritance. Then, the lawyer Qin Liankui stood up and stated the case, stating that the plaintiff's father actually had an inheritance of more than 10 million yuan during his lifetime. After his death, the defendant suddenly claimed that there was only an inheritance of more than 1.5 million yuan. After deducting the costs of funeral and debts, there was little left, which was a huge difference. Last time, the court ordered an audit, but the accountant only extracted a few account books. It should be requested that the court order the defendant to hand over the remaining account books so that the accountant can investigate in detail. Xu Maotang, the defendant, stated that his father's inheritance was actually only 1.56 million. When he made his will, his mother, younger siblings, and others were all present. All the inheritance was managed by his father alone during his lifetime. After his death, his mother held the key to the silver box, so he did not know how much property there was. As for whether there were other account books, the merchant did not know. Then, accountant Xie Lin stated that after being ordered to investigate the accounts of Xu's inheritance, his accountant received 79 account books from the first year of the Republic of China to the 20th year, and a general account book of accumulating gold and jade from the 33rd year of Guangxu to the 19th year of the Republic of China. This general account book was personally recorded by Mr. Xu himself at the end of each year. His accountant believed that Mr. Xu's account books were complete and without any defects. The plaintiff could not force Maotang to hand over other account books. If the plaintiff had any doubts, she could present evidence. At this point, Maotang also stated that on the day before his father died, that is, on the evening of November 10 last year, his younger sister, Meiying, the plaintiff, cried loudly in front of her father, saying, "What will I do after you are gone?" At that time, his father comforted her, saying, "People say that I have tens of millions of assets, but in fact I only have one or two million. Don't listen to other people's words, or get involved in lawsuits," and so on. At that time, the merchant's mother and elder sister were all present and heard it, which could be proved. Finally, after a long debate by the lawyers of both parties, Judge Cao announced the adjournment, and said that he would wait for the accountant to report in detail within fourteen days before making a final decision. On the one hand, he instructed both parties to reconcile out of court.

The Second Special Court Disposes of Huang Chu Jiu's Estate

The Hospital's Marked Price Must Be Above 17,000

The Villa in Hangzhou Cannot Be Disposed of Casually

One-Tenth of the Movable Property Has Been Auctioned

The Disposition of Immovable Property Still Needs Detailed Discussion

The case of the Shanghai Day and Night Bank and the Great World Amusement Savings Department's bankruptcy was collectively investigated by the Second Special District Court yesterday. Judge Cao instructed the lawyers and accountant Pan that today's court session would resolve four matters: (1) Recently, the Shanghai New Medicine Industry Association requested to buy the Huang Chu Jiu Hospital at the previous marked price of 17,000 yuan. I wonder if your lawyers have any opinions on this? The creditor representative, lawyer Yan Luqing, stated that he requested the court to still publish a notice for competitive bidding, and the minimum price must be above 17,000 yuan before it could be sold. Huang's agent lawyer and accountant both expressed their agreement. Judge Cao also said that the second matter was Huang's real estate in Hangzhou. Huang's family and the mortgagee settled the case for more than 10,000 yuan. After investigation, this property is worth more than 20,000 yuan, which is a huge difference. Will it harm the interests of other creditors? What is the method of relief? Lawyer Yan stood up and said that regarding this matter, the former French Public Concession had ordered Huang's family not to dispose of it casually, and ordered it to be transferred to the Shanghai Liquidation Office for joint handling. The settlement is fundamentally invalid and should be relieved. Huang's family agent lawyer Yu Zhongluo stated that according to his lawyer's suggestion, the third creditor must go to the Hangzhou official office to request the revocation of the settlement and continue to handle it according to law to avoid damage. Judge Cao also said that the third matter was that one-tenth of the movable property had already been auctioned. The remaining part must be sold as soon as possible. Is it proper and must be discussed? Accountant Pan sued and made a statement on this point. After the first auction, the Battle of Shanghai occurred before the second auction, which happened during the war and during the lunar New Year. Even if it was auctioned, no one would be interested, so it was stopped. His accountant plans to summarize the accounts at the end of May and then auction them in June when the money market in various places is loose, so as not to suffer losses. The official also said, what about the immovable property? Lawyer Yan and others and the accountant said together, whether the above points can be reported after the lawyers representing the various creditors have discussed them in detail? Judge Cao then approved the request and announced the adjournment.

The Industrial and Commercial Management Association Sees Off Kong Xiangxi

The China Industrial and Commercial Management Association, because its chairman Kong Xiangxi has been appointed as a special envoy to Europe and America for industrial investigation and is about to go abroad, held a banquet yesterday at noon at the Lianhua General Association at 3 Beijing Road to see him off. At the same time, Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo and Mr. Du Chongyuan were invited to speak. Aside from Mr. Chen, who was unable to arrive due to matters in Beijing, over forty people attended, including Association Directors Liu Hongsheng, Xu Jiqing, Li Quanshi, and Director of the International Trade Bureau He Bingxian. Mr. Kong arrived at twelve o'clock. During the banquet, after Chairman Xu Jiqing delivered the opening remarks, Mr. Kong was invited to deliver farewell words, which stated in brief: "I have been ordered to be a special envoy for industrial investigation. When I go abroad, I dare not consider myself a special envoy. I only wish to learn from various countries as a junior apprentice and contribute what I have learned to everyone in the future," etc. Subsequently, Mr. Du Chongyuan delivered a speech on his impressions of investigating the Yangtze River area. The speech was lengthy and is not recorded.

Bank of China Inspection Report

Fiftieth Time

The 50th Inspection Report of the Shanghai Bank of China Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee states: The members of this committee, along with the entrusted accountants, in accordance with the rules of this committee, inspected the Shanghai Bank of China's own issuance and inter-bank withdrawal of convertible note reserve treasury. The 50th inspection was held at the bank on April 24th, 1932, and the Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance joined the inspection. The results of the inspection are listed below: Total amount of convertible notes issued: 10,312,232 yuan, including: 54,592,748 yuan issued by this bank, 20,100,760 yuan withdrawn by inter-bank branches, and 28,421,824 yuan withdrawn by various banks and firms. Except for the portion withdrawn by various banks and firms, which will be inspected separately according to the original method, this inspection covers the inter-bank portion as follows: Amount issued by this bank and withdrawn by inter-bank branches: 74,470,0508 yuan. Amount of convertible note reserve for this bank and inter-bank branches: 74,470,0508 yuan, including: Cash reserve of 45,265,823.57 yuan, and guarantee reserve of 29,434,674.43 yuan. The above two items, calculated as 60% cash reserve and 40% guarantee reserve, were found to be accurate upon inspection. In accordance with Rule 5, this is a formal report. April 24th, 1932. Xu Kan, Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance; Wang Yansong, Pei Yunqing, Representatives of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce; Tang Shoumin, Ye Fuxiao, Representatives of the Shanghai Banking Association; Fu Songnian, Li Jisheng, Representatives of the Shanghai Money Exchange Association; Tang Shoumin, Qi Ziquan, Representatives of the Note-Accepting Banks and Firms; Li Zhilian, Ye Zhuotang, Xu Jiqing, Zhou Zongliang, Representatives of the Directors and Supervisors of the Bank of China; Accountant Wang Zikang.

[P Electricity Turned On in Gaohang Town, Pudong

The Pudong Electric Company extended its lines from Donggou to Gaohang Town. Even though it was during the Japanese invasion, and the situation was dangerous, the work continued as usual and was not interrupted. Now, it is all completed, and the electricity has been turned on. More than 100 households have applied for electric lights. In addition, factories such as cotton ginning and oil pressing plants, which originally used diesel engines, have also converted to motors and applied for connection because the company's electricity prices are low and using electricity is more economical.

Announcement of the Results of the Women's Temperance Society Essay Contest

The 1931 essay contest of the Chinese Women's Temperance Association attracted a large number of submissions due to its novel topic. A total of over 1,000 essays were received. The contest was originally scheduled to be announced in March of this year, but due to the outbreak of the Shanghai War, the members of the association devoted their efforts to comforting and rescuing the victims, which caused a slight suspension of association affairs. Now that the situation is temporarily stable, the work of all departments of the association has gradually resumed. The members of the essay contest committee, including Ms. Liu Wang Liming, have carefully reviewed the essays in recent weeks and held the final judging yesterday. The results were publicly decided as follows: First place: Zheng Youkui from Yenching University, for the essay "The Advantages and Disadvantages of Birth Control," awarded a prize of 50 yuan. Second place: Wu He from National Central University, for the essay "Should Filial Piety be Promoted in the New China?" awarded a prize of 30 yuan. Third place: Xu Xiang from Wuxi Jiangsu Provincial Education Institute, for the essay "The Problem of Beggars in China," awarded a prize of 15 yuan. Fourth place: Hu Ruolin from Nanjing Jinling Theological Seminary, for the essay "Should Filial Piety be Promoted in the New China?" Fifth place: Ms. Ding Liyin from Shanghai, for the essay "The Problem of Beggars in China." Sixth place: Zou Tong from National Central University, for the essay "The Advantages and Disadvantages of Birth Control." Seventh place: Xu Zhangben from Jiaotong University, for the essay "Should Filial Piety be Promoted in the New China?" Eighth place: Sun Shuquan from Jinling Women's University, for the essay "The Advantages and Disadvantages of Birth Control." Ninth place: Qiu Kangle from a law school, for the essay "The Problem of Beggars in China." The above seven names will each receive a prize of 10 yuan, and it is reported that the winners have already been notified by the association with a special letter.

Shanghai West Branch of China Travel Service Sells Shanghai-Suzhou Boat Tickets

The China Travel Service branch on Jing'an Temple Road, Tongfu Road in this port, to facilitate passengers, has reached an agreement with the Yuansheng Inland River Shipping Company to sell various classes of Shanghai-Suzhou boat tickets at prices identical to those of the company, without any additional fees. Official cabins and all other cabins can be reserved to avoid temporary congestion. Other tickets such as train tickets and boat tickets are also sold as usual. Official cabins are 3 yuan per person, room cabins are 5 yuan per room, accommodating three people, third-class cabins are 2 yuan per person, and awning berths are 1.40 yuan per person. The early morning service is at 6:30 AM, and the mid-day service is at 10:00 AM, both arriving in Suzhou on the same day.

[P Weather Report>

Xujiahui Observatory Weather Forecast at 4:30 PM Yesterday: The sky is mostly cloudy over the Shandong coast, the Yangtze River basin, and the coastal areas south of Ma'anshan Island. The wind is gentle and unstable, and there may be fog in the morning in some areas. The typhoon over the Pacific Ocean has reached southwest of the Visayas Islands. Its center was located within 120 miles of the intersection of 7 degrees north latitude and 120 degrees east longitude at noon and will move west or northwest-west. Also, yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the temperature in this port within 24 hours was: highest 80.6, lowest 55.9. On the same day last year, the highest was 57.2 and the lowest was 52.5.

Letter to the Editor

To the Editor: Recently, my client, Chen Wenbin, stated that he was shocked to read in the "Frontline Military News Summary" column of your newspaper on April 23rd that a special dispatch from Suzhou on the 22nd stated that Chen Wenbin had been appointed as a maintenance member after the enemy occupied Liuhe. Mr. Chen himself returned to Wuxi on March 1st, when the enemy invaded Liuhe, and on April 26th, he returned to Liuhe to inspect the goods in his Dachanghe flower shop, staying only one night. There is no truth to the matter of him holding a position as a member of the maintenance committee. It is obvious that someone is deliberately spreading rumors to endanger his life and property. Therefore, I have been specially commissioned by my client to take legal measures to protect him based on the newspaper report. I am writing to request that your newspaper make a correction and publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" section. I would be most grateful. Sincerely, Lawyer Xu Fengbiao, April 26th.

Opening Jumped Up Six Liang and Two Qian From Opening June

3 Liang, 5 Qian and 95 [Wen]

American Cotton Withdrawal

Silk and Tea From Xin and Sheng - Spring Silkworms All Have Silkworm Diseases

Due to Rain-Fed Leaves They Exhibit Symptoms of Yellowing. The Spreading is Very Fast

The Farmers of Xinchan and Sheng Counties Regard Sericulture As An Important Sideline. The Rural Economy Is Withered This Year. The Breeding Scale Has Been Reduced. Early Silkworms Are Already On Their Third Sleep, With Prosperous Leaves. Late Silkworms Are Already On Their Third Sleep As Well. In Recent Days There Has Been Intermittent Rain. Silkworm [Caterpillars] Are Eating Leaves and Growing. Farmers Were Careless. The Silkworms Ate Rain-Fed Leaves, Many Have Symptoms Of Yellowing and Other Diseases. The Spreading Was Very Fast. A Majority Are Being Discarded. This Year's Sericulture Income Will Be Disappointing It Is Said.

Ash-Grey Silk Has Fallen 300 Liang

There Is Only a Market, There Are No Transactions - Sales To America Have Completely Stopped

Yesterday The Shanghai Foreign Firm Silk Market Still Was Not Lively. European and American Firms Regard Chinese Silk As Expensive and Are Not Moving. Ash-Grey Silk Has Fallen From 400 Liang Down To the 300 Liang Price Level, The High Point [Of Speculation] Was At 280 Liang. There Is Only a Market, There Are No Transactions - Sales To America Have Completely Stopped, Factory Management Is Still Holding It Back. The Bad Silk Market of Shanghai Is [An Event] Rare To See In Decades It Is Said.

Qimen Black Tea Is Officially Being Weighed

This Year's Qimen Black Tea Was Cold Most of The Time. The Tea Plant's Development Was Delayed. Recently The Weather Suddenly Turned Hot. The Tea Buds Are Sprouting. All Mountain Farmers Are Rushing The Season and Are Picking Early. Because The Weather Is Clear, The Output Is Good. Different Tea Firms and Local Branches Have Officially Started Weighing The Tea. At Local Pan Village The New Offering Is 80 Yuan Per Dan [Unit]. An Increase of More Than 10 Yuan Compared To Previous Years. At The Southwest Area, The New Offering Is Between 80 to 120 Yuan. An Increase Of Tens Of Yuan Compared To The Previous Increase. The Competition Is Especially Intense at Nan He [Village]. Because Qimen Tea Firms All Converge at Nanlu This Year, If Mountain Farmers' Supply Is Not Strong, Demand Will Exceed Supply. Market Prices Will Continue To Increase.

Wucha Firm Creates Black Tea

Wuyuan Green Tea Has Long Been Known In All The Countries of The World. The Pure and Rich Quality Exceeds Qimen Tea. However, It Has Been A Century of Habits, Known Only For Coloured Green Tea. The Knowledge Of Changing The System Has Not Been Seen. Jinzhu Jitai Teahouse In Yibei, Wuyi [City], Lead By An Owner Named Dan, Utilizes Years of Experience Operating Black Tea In Xiushui Qimen and Is Mining Black Tea in Wuyi Zhuang. The System of Production and Embellishment Are Perfect, and Aesthetic. Mountain Residents Are Being Persuaded to Harvest, At High Prices. Tea Merchants Say Wuyi High Zhuang Mountain Tea Is Extremely Suitable for Making Black Tea, the Leaf Is Better Than Qimen Tea. This Trial Will Surely Bear Successful Results.

Free Talk

Japanese Military Pigeon Straying to Chongming

— Rong

A farmer named Zhao from Xinkai River in Chongming raises dozens of pigeons at home. A few days ago, a strange pigeon suddenly appeared among his flock. Its shape was sturdy and unlike ordinary pigeons. Zhao then used food as bait and devised a plan to capture it. Upon inspection, he found a soft tin tube tied to its leg, as thin as a chopstick and about an inch long. The end of the tube had a spiral cap. When he opened it, he found a piece of foreign text. Zhao was a local and did not even know Chinese, let alone a foreign language. He asked his neighbors, but they were all dumbfounded and did not know. The matter was learned by County Magistrate Shen of the county, who immediately telephoned the district office to buy it from Zhao for ten yuan and quickly send it to the county government for research. County Magistrate Shen was proficient in Eastern languages and translated it in detail. Only then did he learn that it was a military intelligence report sent by the Japanese army from Liuhe to Shanghai. The Chinese meaning was that the Liuhe area lacked horse feed, soldiers were mostly sick, and they were unwilling to fight, and so on. Shen immediately reported it to the provincial government and forwarded it to the military authorities for verification.

Newspaper Talk Odds and Ends

— Songlu

When I was a child, I studied under Mr. Chen Langru. Mr. Chen and my late father were close friends. They jointly subscribed to one copy of the Shen Bao. At that time, transportation in my hometown was blocked. Only two or three newspapers were subscribed to in the entire town. Every day, I would deliver the newspaper that my father had read to Mr. Chen. I did this throughout the year without interruption. I was so loyal to this job that I was almost a newspaper boy.

It was difficult to get newspapers in remote villages, and the villagers could not even read them. However, they always had a Shen Bao in their minds. Whenever they saw a large printed item, they would say it was Shen Bao paper. It was rare, and therefore the value of the newspaper was even more precious. My family subscribed to one newspaper, and people constantly came to the door asking for old newspapers. Giving away a few sheets would often result in them being used to patch up broken walls, mixed up and upside down, without regard for order. The lack of popularization of culture in our country can be seen from this.

The newspaper is a representation of the times, but its power is also sufficient to transform the times. The Shen Bao over the past sixty years has advocated for civil rights and constitutionalism, and has made some contributions to the founding of the Republic of China. However, even today, although the revolution has been completed, civil rights have not yet been realized. What the Shen Bao should strive for is even more unrelenting.

A Split-Character's Words

— Yunjian Poor Knight

Zheng Shiwei from Hunan is eloquent and penniless. Every day, he relies on split-character analysis in various teahouses in Rongcheng to make a living. His speech is like a waterfall, and his words are subtle and to the point. Therefore, his life is not so lonely. Yesterday, I saw him analyzing the character "party" for a young man in Wangjiang Tower. First, he asked the young man what it was for. The young man said he was asking about current events. Zheng then opened the floodgates and spoke volubly, saying, "Looking at the shape of the character 'party', it is quite like rules and uprightness, without party or bias. However, the top of the character 'party' is the character 'small,' which looks like a fat, dark person wearing a melon-skin pointed hat, somewhat like a fashionable singer. In the end, it feels like a pointed-head trick. Moreover, the character 'above' is '尙,' which occupies four-tenths of the entire character. Below is the character 'black,' which occupies six-tenths of the entire character. In the end, the black atmosphere is too heavy and not very noble. Even if we take the character '尙,' removing the character 'small,' it becomes '回.' If you add a small stroke to the character '口,' it becomes the character '同.' I am afraid of opening the door to party-spirit and suppressing differences, and I am even more afraid of the phenomenon of being the same without harmony. Moreover, there is only the character '口' in the character '尙,' and I am especially afraid of falling into the trap of saying one thing and thinking another, having a mouth but no heart. Again, if we take the character 'small,' its meaning is small, but what is related to it is huge. If you add a stroke below the character 'small,' it becomes the character '少.' In recent years, there have been many happy events, and many are full of vigor. I am deeply afraid of inexperience, leading to a huge disaster. If a disaster breaks out, the common people will suffer undeserved misfortune, and the overall situation will also suffer damage. Therefore, no matter how big or small the event, it is always best to be careful and cautious. Even if you feel extremely painful in your heart, you must remain extremely peaceful on the surface. At this time, when villains are gaining power, we must never show the slightest sign of anger in our words or expressions. If we do, perhaps we can turn big things into small things and small things into nothing. If we take the character 'black,' it is now a time when black and white are confused, not when black and white are distinct. There are many black hearts and few red hearts. Most of the world's humans have black eyes and only see silver. Even if there are enlightened people, they are mostly shrouded in a huge black atmosphere and there is nothing they can do. In short, it is simply not a dark world, but has become a dark hell. To seek a ray of light from this and break this black lacquer lantern, it will not be successful without the concerted effort of everyone from top to bottom." The young man reached into his pocket and took out two dimes to pay him. Zheng then thanked him and left.

World Little Things Record

— Haike

London, the capital of England, is often foggy and rainy. During the most recent three and a half months of dark skies, theft cases have occurred frequently. There have been as many as 479 cases of handbags being snatched from pedestrians on the street.

The authorities in southern France, in order to change the road policy, felt that the white roads, although beautiful, are too dazzling under sunlight. Therefore, they plan to completely change all the roads to red. Other second-class roads will be changed to green and yellow.

Many dogs are being trained in German asylums for the deaf and dumb to serve deaf and dumb people. They are taught to recognize various required signals. For example, when the dog is walking with its owner on the street, as soon as it hears the sound of a car horn, it can warn its owner in advance to avoid being hit.

Americans love movies the most. According to a recent survey, there are a total of 20,500 movie theaters in the country, with a total of 18.6 million seats. In all of Europe (excluding Russia), there are only 27,000 movie theaters with only 11 million seats.

Record of Double Buildings of the Military Horses (39)

— Seeking Happiness Studio Owner

Chapter Five: Forsaking Loyalty and Breaking Off Friendship; Unfortunately, Meeting a Wealthy Guest; Angrily Closing off the Heart; Devising a Strategy; Most Difficult to Endure the Kindness of a Beauty

He then answered excitedly, "I want to struggle alone and find my own way. Originally, it was useless for me to study politics and law in college. Now that soldiers are in charge, doing anything is better than being a military officer. While I don't have money to go to school, I might as well change careers early and join the army. I heard that Military Governor Ye Zuozhang in my provincial capital is making every effort to expand the army and has newly established a military academy to recruit students. I plan to go back and take the exam. First, I can use it as a place to settle down and maintain my livelihood. Second, after graduating, I can become a junior military officer and do my best to seek a future and develop. If heaven wills it, one day I will also be able to grasp great military power. I vow to severely suppress the bandits and kill Niu Heifeng to avenge my parents." Liang Xiaoyun heard this and took a puff of her cigarette. She couldn't help but chuckle and said, "I can't see that you have such great ambition. It's just a pity that it sounds like a child talking in his sleep. In today's cold and fickle world, no matter what you do in any military or political field, without someone to specifically promote you or without strong support, it is impossible to have good hope by blindly breaking through with your own little skills. You're going to be a student in a military academy, spending all your efforts and graduating in three years. At most, you'll only be a platoon or company commander. Hoping to be promoted step by step from this basic junior officer to become a division or brigade commander, with great military power in hand, so that you can eliminate Niu Heifeng, is truly more difficult than ascending to heaven. I'm afraid that by the time your hair turns white, you'll still be selling your strength in vain and just dreaming. You'll never achieve your purpose. Your plan is too clumsy." An Yutian was greatly discouraged by her ridicule and answered dejectedly, "What you say is certainly very insightful, but I have no other way to go. I can only be like a monk cultivating diligently, muddling through step by step." Liang Xiaoyun smiled and said, "I don't quite agree with your cowardly idea of leaving everything to fate. Moreover, things depend on human effort. I don't believe there's nothing to be done. In my opinion, your idea is not necessarily wrong. Although you may not be able to make it alone, there are many capable people in the world. Isn't there a reliable friend who can help you?" An Yutian quickly asked, "Who are you teaching me to ask for help from?" Liang Xiaoyun smiled and pointed to her nose carved like beautiful jade and said, "Right in front of you. Why didn't you think of me?" An Yutian was suddenly startled and then asked, "What good idea do you have?"

Commemorative Matters

— Buddha

In a certain period, when a shocking event suddenly occurs, this event must be easily remembered in people's minds and easily unforgettable forever. Yesterday, I wrote a small piece of history in the supplement, describing the time I entered Shen Bao for the second time. My brother Yunhe saw it and was very suspicious. I said it was correct. He said why? I said I have a surprising fact that can be used as evidence, which is the assassination of the Manchu Governor Enming by Xu Xilin. I also published Xu Xilin's book to worship Duke Xu, and I also gained a lot of rights. Is this thing not tragic and violent enough to make me forget it from my mind?

In Mr. Ma's article "Sixty Years in Shanghai," which was added to the supplement, it also mentioned the interesting anecdote of Kang Shengren owing a debt for prostitution. At that time, Kang had no way to pay, so he closed his eyes and came up with a plan. He immediately jumped into the rescue boat, and a pile of dirty debts was actually paid off cleanly. Although Mr. Ma has a strong memory, he is already ninety-three years old this year. I don't know how many strange things he has experienced. Kang Shengren has been dead for many years. This fragrant and interesting history must be a thirty-year-old story, because Mr. Ma believes that this story is very interesting and valuable, so he keeps it in his mind and has not forgotten it until now. Yesterday was the 60th anniversary of this newspaper, and I re-mentioned the tragic and violent assassination of Enming by Xu Xilin. Mr. Ma Xiangbo mentioned Kang Shengren's romantic anecdotes. This kind of special and interesting thing is unforgettable, and because of the 60th anniversary of this newspaper, mentioning this matter is even more unforgettable. Alas! Don't forget the 60th anniversary of this newspaper.

[P Scientific Adhesives

— Huang Wei

Leather, paper, wood, and glass are commonly bonded with glue. However, these types of adhesives lose their effectiveness when exposed to water. Shellac flakes are not wetted by water and are excellent adhesives. They can be used for both metal and non-metal objects. Heat the shellac flakes and add a small amount of alcohol to dissolve them before use.

There are several types of adhesives for glass. Shellac flakes are one of them. This type of adhesive can only prevent water from entering. If used in alcohol, it loses its effectiveness. Therefore, chemical labs and pharmacies often have no choice but to use imported adhesives. However, if you take a small amount of rubber tubing, heat it and dissolve it, and then add carbon disulfide until it becomes a thin liquid, you can apply this liquid to the area to be bonded. Its effectiveness is no different from imported products.

Sodium silicate is the best adhesive for glass and metal. Its strength is unmatched by other types of adhesives.

The above types of glass adhesives are all effective in commercial use and each has its own advantages. However, if you want to bond glass to glass and make it transparent, you must use Canadian balsam. Many bulletproof glasses are made of numerous very thin pieces of glass bonded together with this adhesive.

Artificial ivory is a compound of guncotton and camphor. There are many products on the market recently. The white panels of organs and pianos, children's toys, etc. are all made of it. If you want to bond it, you can take a small piece of artificial ivory and dissolve it in acetone before using it to bond objects.

Forging bonding to bonding seems the same but is actually different. The medication must wait for a separate topic and discussion.

East West North South

One-Sided Views on National Salvation Plans

— I

Since China has had national disasters, I have intentionally or unintentionally read quite a few national salvation plans from scholars and celebrities.

Another national salvation plan! Another national salvation plan!

However, can these plans really save the country? Although this is still a question (sorry! gentlemen, I apologize!), this can be largely ignored, why? Because that is at least a "concrete plan" with thoughtful consideration. At the very least, the drafter himself can completely believe in its "existence," right?

Some advocate a one-party dictatorship. —They say this is the advocacy of nationalism.

Some advocate restoring relations with the Soviet Union. —They say this is the view of the left. (According to Chinese law, this has the suspicion of being a communist party.)

Some say align with the United States. —Which faction's advocacy is this?

Some say always believe in the League of Nations. —Which faction's advocacy is this? ... And so on.

Justice is upright. All roads lead to Rome.

Of course, when there is a "national disaster" one must "save the country," which is the unanimous voice of patriotic people. For example, during the European War, the German government and celebrities all advocated "fighting for the glory of the motherland." When the Soviet Union encountered an attack by the great powers, it also incited the workers to "support the workers' motherland." Even this time, the Japanese also shouted "open up the national disaster!" and also "maintain the special rights and dignity of this empire," and did not hesitate to send heavy troops to "punish Chinese warlords." (Note carefully, the tone is extremely clever!) In this way, there is no doubt that the "country" should be "saved," what remains is the way to save the country.

In this way, these grand articles are extremely useful. Alas! Magnificent!

However, those who implement the plan are out there, are they willing to "prescribe according to the law" according to the "prescription" of the gentlemen? Otherwise, to implement it, one must first "govern." Then, if you are in power, are you willing to do it impartially without betraying your previous words? Do you not plan for your own "interests" at all? This is hard to say.

As for having the hope of governing or even crossing the threshold of an official yamen after first coming up with a national salvation plan, this should be an inevitable truth.

Moreover, the so-called national disaster is not necessarily only the Anti-Japanese War, just like the scope of discussion prescribed by the Luoyang National Disaster Conference. Therefore, scholars and celebrities! You must hurry to include "appeasement..." in your plan, otherwise it will not be easy to realize the rejoicing of the gentlemen in the future, right?

A Corner of Society

Two Impressions

— Gan Fang

The sound of artillery is far away, the school bell rings. I can't believe that I can still be educated when my motherland is dying. I'm almost crazy with joy carrying my schoolbag.

This is the new school site. The school building is small, and there is not even a rest room. After class, I wandered alone on the sunbathing platform, because I was transferred here during this school's big sale. I didn't know a single strange person. I opened the book boredly, half spread on the railing and half in my hand. I can't see the playground, laughing, fighting, making a lot of noise. Four or five people sat in a circle near the playground, and they were all holding small, long-style cards in their hands. The red plum blossoms deeply attracted my attention. I knew they were playing poker.

I hurried to class, the bell had already rung, and I squeezed into the classroom, but there were no seats left. An unfamiliar classmate gave up half of his seat for me. The short and dark teacher was lecturing on "differentiation of characters." Two minutes later, he suddenly stopped. "Please don't smoke in class! The classroom is too small, the number of people is too large, and the air is no longer clean. It's too heartbreaking to mention these things—our own spacious lecture hall has been occupied by others." His eyelids fluttered faster, and he spoke sincerely and sadly to the classmate in the back row who was smoking. But he also felt that it was too embarrassing for him to say this, so he quickly covered up and said, "I am also a smoking king, I just don't smoke in the classroom."

What time is this? The cannons haven't stopped, the soldiers haven't retreated, the national hatred hasn't been avenged. We are young people, how can this ambition be relaxed? But the first impression given to me was so, making my hot blood run cold from head to toe. I knew that this was the achievement of university education! When I write here, I sincerely hope that our leaders, especially those who run university education, should not talk empty words of saving the country, the education received is not suitable for today, this group of half-fallen young people, this group of future masters of China, if not thoroughly reformed and strictly trained, let them be free and unrestrained again, then we are ready to see China perish! Conscience compels me to petition my dear teachers with blood and tears.

Market News

Miss Xu Shumei, who won first place in the Shanghai Shih Pao newspaper trademark competition, and her sisters Renmeilu Zhi, etc., founded a Women's Livelihood Cooperative. The general affairs and sewing departments have now been established at the bottom of Hongqingli, Xinzha Road. Experienced Chinese and Western technicians have been hired to recruit female students, teaching machine sewing and tailoring. All work is supplied by the cooperative to promote women's industry with a relief nature. Since its establishment, it has been well received by society, with various sectors eagerly sending clothes, flags, and tents due to the cheap labor costs.

Jiangsu High Court Second Branch

Criminal Judgments

One case of Liu Jiu vs. Huang Bingyan and others, accused of fraud (Main Text): The original judgment regarding the order for the appellants to jointly compensate the full amount to the appellees is revoked. The appellees' lawsuit against one appellant in the first instance is dismissed.

▲One case of Chen Zheng and others, accused of collecting enticed persons with intent to profit (Main Text): The appeal is dismissed.

▲One case of Liu Jiugao vs. Huang Bingyan and others, accused of fraud (Main Text): The original judgment regarding Liu Jiu's crime and punishment is revoked. Liu Jiu is found not guilty.

▲One case of Tong Sanmao, also known as Tong Wenbo, accused of abetting suicide (Main Text): The original judgment is revoked. Tong Sanmao is acquitted of abetting suicide.

▲One case of Peng Xia (wife of Peng Ajin), regarding Peng Ajin's robbery appeal (Main Text): The original judgment regarding Peng Ajin is revoked. Peng Ajin is sentenced to three years and six months imprisonment for joint theft. The number of days in detention before the final judgment shall be offset against the prison term at a rate of two days for one day. One pistol and six bullets are confiscated.

▲One case of Kress vs. She Fei, regarding an appeal for trademark infringement (Main Text): The original judgment is revoked and remanded to the Shanghai First Special District Court for retrial.

Civil Judgments

The petitioner Wang Jincheng vs. Xu Zhenyu, regarding a dispute over a guarantee debt appeal (Main Text): The appeal and petition are both dismissed. The appellants shall bear the costs of the second instance litigation and petition.

▲One case of petitioner Lin Shifa vs. Lin Weirong, regarding a dispute over goods (Main Text): The petitioner shall bear the petition fees.

▲One case of the National Government Restructuring China Merchants Bureau General Administration vs. Yuanchang Kun Kee, regarding a dispute over repayment of goods appeal (Main Text): The appeal is dismissed. The appellants shall bear the costs of the second instance litigation.

▲One case of She Pei vs. Anderson Meyer & Co. Lasso, regarding an appeal for compensation (Main Text): The appeal is dismissed. The appellants shall bear the costs of the second instance litigation.

April 30th Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special District Court

▲Criminal Judgments

Police Department vs. Qin Dafu, opium case (Main Text): Qin Dafu is fined one hundred yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If unable to pay, two yuan will be converted to one day of imprisonment. The number of days in detention before the final judgment shall be offset against the fine at a rate of one day for two yuan. The opium pipe, lamp, needle, and tray are all confiscated and burned.

▲Police Department vs. Chen Guihua and others, obstructing official duties case (Main Text): Chen Guihua and Chen Guifu are both found not guilty.

▲Private prosecutor Zheng Caibao vs. Shao Mutao, for issuing a bad check case (Main Text): This case is not accepted.

▲Police Department vs. Zhao Gaofeng and others, theft case (Main Text): Zhao Gaofeng is sentenced to one year imprisonment for habitual theft. Nie Xiru and Liu Xinzhi are each sentenced to six months imprisonment for theft committed by a group of three or more. The number of days in detention before the final judgment shall be offset against the prison term at a rate of two days for one day. Nie Xiru and Liu Xinzhi are each given a three-year suspended sentence.

▲Police Department vs. Fu Bingjun and others, opium case (Main Text): Fu Bingjun is sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined two hundred yuan for providing his premises for others to use opium. Liu Gen and A Gen are sentenced to two months imprisonment for smoking opium. Ge Weibao, Zhu Xijun, and Ding Wenhua are each sentenced to one month imprisonment and fined one hundred yuan for smoking opium. If unable to pay the fine, two yuan will be converted to one day of imprisonment. The number of days in detention before the final judgment shall be offset against the prison term at a rate of two days for one day. Jin Didan, Sun Jin, and Jin Shun are found not guilty. The opium pipe and other items are confiscated and burned according to the list.

The number of days in detention before the final judgment shall be offset against the prison term at a rate of two days for one day. Zhang Zaibao, Cao Heshang, and Chen Dejin are each given a two-year suspended sentence. The opium pipe and red pills are confiscated and burned according to the list.

Civil Judgments

Yang Tingzhang vs. Rong Bingjun and others, deposit case (Main Text): The defendant Rong Bingjun shall repay the plaintiff 230 yuan and pay overdue interest at a monthly rate of 1.5% from August 10, 1931, until the date of final execution. The defendant Yu Yongfu shall repay the plaintiff 150 yuan and pay interest at a monthly rate of 1.5% from June 1931 until the date of final execution. The plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed. The plaintiff shall bear one-third of the litigation costs, and the defendants shall bear two-thirds.

▲Zhang Shutian vs. Wei Maogou, loan case (Main Text): The payment order issued by this court on November 24, 1931, is upheld. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs.

▲Commercial Printing House vs. Mahler, goods case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 98 yuan and interest at an annual rate of 5% from September 28, 1931, until the date of final execution. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs.

▲Darley vs. Chen Zheming, rent arrears case (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff rent of 108 yuan and 9 jiao. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs.

▲Shanghai Banking Corporation vs. Bertleski and others, bill case (Main Text): The defendants shall jointly pay the plaintiff's bill amount of 312 yuan and a loss fee of 50 taels of silver. The defendants shall jointly bear the litigation costs.

▲Senderlegov vs. Miao Ming, debt case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 295.40 Japanese yen and interest at an annual rate of 5% from the date of the lawsuit until the date of final execution. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs.

▲Dong Fanggao vs. Lin Baohua, deposit and compensation case (Main Text): The petition is dismissed. The petitioner shall bear the petition fees.

▲Longfei Co., Ltd. Liquidation Office Tong Geluo Kaofu vs. Fan Hengde and others, debt case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim against the defendant Fan Hengde is dismissed. The defendant Xie Tuying should pay the plaintiff 78 taels, 1 qian, 8 fen of silver and 121 yuan. The plaintiff shall bear five-eighths of the litigation costs, and the defendant Xie Tuying shall bear two-eighths.

▲Li Miermen vs. Piliyani and others, goods case (Main Text): The plaintiff's lawsuit is dismissed. The plaintiff shall bear the litigation costs.

▲Lu Xingen vs. Lu Linsheng, property division case (Main Text): The plaintiff's lawsuit is dismissed. The plaintiff shall bear the litigation costs.

▲Ni Jiangfu vs. Tongji Ice Company, goods appeal case (Main Text): The appeal is dismissed. The appellant shall bear the litigation costs of the second instance (above is for April 30th).

▲Civil Instructions

One case of Lu Xihou petitioning for auction. As per the statement, the Yad Automobile of the debtor, National Automobile Company, was previously sealed by this court. Subsequently, according to the statement of Yad Automobile Company, the price of the automobile has not been fully paid, and an objection is made requesting that it not be sold. After this court dispatched personnel to appraise it together with the Dahua Auction Company, it was confirmed that the automobile's engine number is 1977241, which matches the number submitted by Yad Automobile Company in its objection. The auction should be stopped. You should be informed of this instruction.

▲One case of the French Concession Police Department petitioning for the removal of a wall foundation. As per the statement, after investigating this case, a court hearing was held, and the attorney Gu Shou, the agent of the Municipal Council's Engineering Department, stated that the encroaching part of Lu Yongnian's property had been removed on February 15. Now, according to the statement, after investigation by the Municipal Council, it is confirmed that the foundation of the house has not been removed. The request that the Municipal Council remove it on its behalf should be approved. This instruction.

▲One case of Ted Beck petitioning for enforcement. As per the statement, the files of this case have not yet been returned after appeal review. The requested action should be delayed. This instruction (April 30th).

Shanghai District Court

▲Criminal Judgments

Li Mingzhong and others, theft case (Main Text): Li Mingzhong and Wang Zhenchuan are found not guilty. Yu Jinxin, Hou Afa, Yao Wenming, and Xie Xiaowen are each sentenced to six months imprisonment for theft committed during a disaster.

▲Zhang Chen and others, opium case (Main Text): Zhang Chen is fined 120 yuan for possessing opium substitutes with the intention of committing a crime. If the fine cannot be paid through compulsory enforcement, one yuan will be converted to one day of imprisonment. The number of days in detention shall be offset against the fine at a rate of one day for one yuan. Wang Sijiu and Huang Jinfu are both found not guilty. Twenty-seven red pills, a bottle, three opium pipes, two bamboo poles, two opium lamps, one opium tray, and two opium holders are all confiscated and burned.

▲Shen Zhongxin, theft and opium case (Main Text): Shen Zhongxin is sentenced to six months imprisonment for committing theft during an emergency. The number of days in detention shall be offset against the prison term at a rate of two days for one day. Shen Zhongxin is found not guilty on the opium charge.

▲Lu Fulin and others, theft case (Main Text): Lu Fulin and Yu Min are each sentenced to two months imprisonment for joint theft. The number of days in detention shall be offset against the prison term at a rate of two days for one day.

▲Cai Jinyuan and others, occupation of lost property case (Main Text): Cai Jinbiao is sentenced to three months imprisonment for occupying property that he held in his work and that belonged to others, with the intent of illegally possessing it. The number of days in detention shall be offset against the prison term at a rate of two days for one day. Mu Fuyuan is sentenced to twenty days of detention for buying stolen goods. The number of days in detention shall be offset against the detention period at a rate of two days for one day.

▲Li Afu and others, murder case (Main Text): Li Afu is sentenced to twelve years imprisonment for joint murder and is permanently deprived of civil rights. The number of days in detention shall be offset against the prison term at a rate of two days for one day. The trials of Lu Ru, An Yu, Fei Hong, Jin Hong, and Fang Jiu are suspended.

▲Fang Jibo, assault appeal case (Main Text): The appeal is dismissed.

▲Sun Zhenfa and others, stolen goods case (Main Text): Sun Zhenfa, Yang Decai, Wei Daifu, and Le Changqi are each sentenced to three months imprisonment for jointly harboring stolen goods. The number of days in detention shall be offset against the prison term at a rate of two days for one day.

▲Li Fusheng, robbery case (Main Text): Li Fusheng is found not guilty.

▲Xun Zhaogang, disturbing the family case (Main Text): Xun Zhaogang is sentenced to six months imprisonment for having intercourse with a woman under the age of twenty with the intent to commit adultery. The number of days in detention shall be offset against the prison term at a rate of two days for one day.

▲Luo Bin, assault case (Main Text): Luo Bin is sentenced to four years and eight months imprisonment for assault causing death. The number of days in detention shall be offset against the prison term at a rate of two days for one day.

▲Xiao Xunyang, theft and public endangerment case (Main Text): Xiao Xunyang is sentenced to one year and six months imprisonment for damaging signs, resulting in the danger of train traffic, attempted. The number of days in detention shall be offset against the prison term at a rate of two days for one day.

▲Chen Zongbo, opium case (Main Text): Chen Zongbo is sentenced to six months imprisonment for transporting opium with the intention of selling it. The number of days in detention shall be offset against the prison term at a rate of two days for one day. Seven taels of raw opium and three taels and five qian of opium ash are confiscated and burned.

▲Ni Fengxiang, opium case (Main Text): Ni Fengxiang is sentenced to six months imprisonment for intending to transport opium and is fined fifty yuan. If the fine cannot be paid through compulsory enforcement, one yuan will be converted to one day of imprisonment. The number of days in detention shall be offset against the prison term at a rate of two days for one day. Fifty-four taels of raw opium are confiscated and burned.

The plaintiff's lawsuit against the defendants Su Yingjie and Xu Tongxiang is dismissed.

If Ge Qixiang is unable to repay, the defendant Luo Guisheng shall be responsible for substitute repayment. The defendant Ge Qixiang shall bear the litigation costs.

The appellant's appeal and the remaining claims of the appellees in the first instance are dismissed. The appellant shall bear six-tenths of the litigation costs for the first, second, and previous third instances, and the appellees shall jointly bear four-tenths.

▲Tao Lianggong vs. Zhenxing Automobile Company and others, goods case (Main Text): The defendant Jiang Qingyi shall repay the plaintiff's goods payment of 109 yuan and 3 jiao. If unable to repay, Qi Renlin shall bear the substitute repayment. Jiang Qingyi shall bear the litigation costs.

▲Chunyuan Company vs. Zhu Boman, rent case (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 533 yuan, 4 jiao, 5 fen, and 96 jiao. Except for the one-quarter of the litigation costs for the withdrawn part, which is borne by the plaintiff, the remaining three-quarters shall be borne by the defendant.

▲Wu Anlin vs. Min Zhengqing and others, objection to execution case (Main Text): The productive property of the American-Luen Printing Bureau in question shall be returned to the plaintiff to resume business as before, and shall not be available for execution in the case of Min Zhengqing and Chen Jinshen's breach of contract. The defendant Min Zhengqing shall bear the litigation costs.

▲Guo Zhang vs. Zhang Pan, handover and alimony case (Main Text): The previous judgment is reversed. The defendants shall pay the plaintiff a monthly fee of 6 yuan from February 1930 until the date of final execution. The plaintiff's claim regarding the handover of the field certificate is dismissed. The plaintiff shall bear two-thirds of the litigation costs for this trial and the previous second instance, and the defendants shall bear one-third. The second item of this judgment shall be subject to provisional execution.

▲Dai Zuopei vs. Ying Guoping, bill case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 1,200 yuan, with 600 yuan bearing interest at an annual rate of 5% from September 6, 1930, and another 600 yuan bearing interest at an annual rate of 5% from October 6 of the same year, until the date of final execution. The defendant shall bear nineteen-twentieths of the litigation costs, and the plaintiff shall bear one-twentieth.

▲Zhang Tingzhen vs. Wang Dianchen, compensation for injury case (Main Text): The defendant shall compensate the plaintiff for losses of 1,500 yuan. The plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed. The defendant shall bear three-quarters of the litigation costs, and the plaintiff shall bear one-quarter.
