Unconventional Comfort Items

— Cang

This Shanghai war, which has aroused global sympathy and is fought for the survival of our nation, has yet to bring us, the people, to a final victory. However, the general public has been very enthusiastic in offering comfort to our loyal and brave armed comrades who are fighting for the glory of the nation. Besides money, countless other military supplies and necessities have been provided. Among these many comfort items, three are particularly noteworthy and unbelievable. First, an American gave five US dollars as a token of comfort. He also included a letter with many words of admiration. At the end, he said that five dollars was not enough to distribute to all the brothers, but he hoped that they could buy a few bullets to resist the inhuman enemy.

Second, overseas Chinese from Southeast Asia sent two book coupons from the Commercial Press, worth only two yuan and two jiao. In their letter, they also said that this was not enough to comfort them, but asked them to buy a few more bullets.

Third, someone sent a mandarin jacket as a gesture of comfort, without explaining its intention, which was baffling. Aren't the above three comfort items unconventional?

Random Talk

Who is the Traitor?

— Bai Tao

A few days ago, newspapers published a letter from Mr. Xiong Xiling to President Wang Jingwei, stating that President Wang had said during the Central Memorial Week that Mr. Xiong was a co-signer of the Twenty-One Demands and a traitor! He is now in Shanghai, and if he comes to Luoyang to attend the National Crisis Conference, we will kill him! Therefore, Mr. Xiong defended himself, saying that although he had served as the Prime Minister of the State Council in the fourth year of the Republic of China, he had already resigned when the Twenty-One Demands, a treaty of national betrayal, were signed. He asked President Wang to verify the official records before speaking. He also respectfully advised President Wang that, at a time of national crisis, those in important positions must be cautious for the sake of the country. We, the common people, do not wish to criticize the rights and wrongs of you gentlemen, but it is indeed true that Mr. Xiong was not a co-signer of the Twenty-One Demands, a treaty of national betrayal. Then, who is the traitor who signed the treaty of national betrayal?

It is none other than the notorious traitor Lu Zengxiang, one of the three great traitors Cao, Lu, and Zhang. It is said that Lu Zengxiang, feeling remorseful for signing the treaty of national betrayal, has abandoned his family and gone abroad to become a monk!

At this time of national crisis, these old accounts can be ignored. If we were to settle old scores, I fear that the accounting would be more harmful than beneficial. However, "before old debts are settled, hold your tongue." Although old accounts can be ignored, new ones must not be added. When a nation is about to perish, there will be demons. If, at this time, we do not produce Yue Fei but instead produce many more Qin Huis, what will we do? I advise the common people not to let go of traitors!

Movies

After Watching "Romance"

Recently, "Romance", this year's colossal film starring Greta Garbo and Ruth Chatterton, who have once again been crowned as movie queens, has been released at the Nanjing Grand Theatre. It is a masterpiece that combines sorrow, humor, and music in one. In this world, things are rarely as one wishes, and most people are heartbroken. Chatterton in the film is no exception. If lovers could always be together, the joy of companionship would be self-evident. Alas, heaven is unkind, burning the zither and boiling the crane, causing endless sorrow and grief. Ah, Chatterton's performance is delicate, profound, and deeply moving. The comedic star, Arnold Korff, already left us with a deep impression with his performance in "Transatlantic". Now, he interjects hilarious jokes into the film, allowing us to find some joy in sorrow. His adjustment is especially good. The film is purely musical and artistic, featuring six new songs composed by Herbert Stothart, a major modern American composer. The lyrics are profound and extraordinary, and they are paired with beautiful music. The supporting actress, Clara Blandick, has a bold and flamboyant style. This film opened at the largest Loews Theatre in the United States and broke all previous box office records, not by chance.

Carlton Shows "Private Lives"

"Private Lives," which is showing at the Carlton, is a superb film selected from hundreds of British films. Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer, the largest film company in the United States, spent a large sum of money to acquire the exclusive screening rights for the film in the United States. When it premiered in the United States, all the viewers praised it unanimously. The success in box office broke all records. This film is not only tightly plotted, but also has an excellent structure, which is rare because it does not fall into the usual clichés. As for the star of this film, she is a London stage star who is famous for a time. Her performance is so realistic that it can bring tears to the eyes.

"Heartbroken Flower" Coming Soon

A weak woman. She wants to move upward with all her heart. But the unfortunate fate, the adverse environment, and the criticism of society all want to drive her into hell. This is such a heartbreaking thing. That is why the film "Heartbroken Flower" is able to make people shed tears. The "Heartbroken Flower" in the film was originally a very virtuous girl from a humble family. But that unfortunate fate followed her every step of the way, causing her to live a life of wretchedness. And for helping her beloved son to become famous, she did not hesitate to sacrifice her beauty and engage in the profession of selling laughter. As a result, although her beloved son was fortunately successful, she was devastated. In short, from beginning to end, this film can be said to have scene after scene of blood and word after word of tears. Needless to say, emotional people will be moved to tears by it, and even those with hearts of stone will shed tears after watching it. There is also one thing that is most rare, that is, the leading actress, Helen Twelvetrees, plays the roles of four different eras, and they are all lifelike. Her makeup skills and performance ability are not something that can be accomplished without artistic talent. It is said that this film will soon be released at the Cathay Theatre.
